```#include <iostream>

void printPositiveValues(int a, int b) {
    if (a > 0) {
        std::cout << "Positive value of a: " << a << std::endl;
    }
    if (b > 0) {
        std::cout << "Positive value of b: " << b << std::endl;
    }
}

int main() {
    int x = 10;
    int y = -5;

    printPositiveValues(x, y);

    return 0;
}```
